######################################
###House Baratheon Anchien history.###
###Added by Chrismj89 in Colaboration with Oga
###Ours is the Fury!##################

#Done the Baratheon family tree. Not the cadet branches of Bolling and Wensington yet though. Rhaelle and the Lannister patriarchs have been updated/corrected too.
#I've added charinfo and a new house 'Godsgrief' its the same CoA of Baratheon so that will be easy. Bolling and Wensington have separate CoA. They are on the wiki though.

#- House Baratheon - House Godsgrief. Founders of Bolling and Wensington. \Update/ Godsgrief now Durrandon.
#Plus connections. Targaryen and Lannister.

1317 = {
	name= "Orys"  # Baratheon rumoured half-brother of Aegon the Conqueror.
	dynasty=498
	
	dna="bfcfecbikdk"
	properties="ac0ack"
	
	martial = 13
	diplomacy = 8
	intrigue = 4
	stewardship = 10
	learning = 6

	religion="valyrian"
	culture="western_valyrian"

	add_trait="bastard"
	add_trait="strong"
	add_trait="honorable"
	
	father=77064
	employer=77064

	7978.1.1 = {
		birth="7978.1.1" 
		add_trait=assign_mission_target #cadet dynasty tracker, baratheon
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { dynasty = 317 } }
				set_dynasty_flag = is_cadet_house
				c_77064 = { #targaryen father
					set_dynasty_flag = has_cadet_house
					set_dynasty_flag = owned_cadet_house_@PREV
					ROOT = { set_dynasty_flag = cadet_house_@PREV }
				}
			}	
		}
	}	
	7987.1.1 = {add_trait="gregarious"}
	7991.1.1 =  {add_trait="authoritative"}	
	7994.1.1 = {add_trait="skilled_tactician"
	            add_trait="duelist"
			    add_trait="master_warrior"
			    add_trait="brave"}

			}

						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8130 } }

							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
